\documentclass{extarticle}
\usepackage[utf8]{inputenc}
\usepackage{amsmath}
\usepackage{pgfplots}
\usepackage{tikz}
\usepackage{pgfplotstable}

\pgfplotsset{
  discard if/.style 2 args={
    x filter/.code={
      \edef\tempa{\thisrow{#1}}
      \edef\tempb{#2}
      \ifx\tempa\tempb
      \def\pgfmathresult{inf}
      \fi
    }
  },
  discard if not/.style 2 args={
    x filter/.code={
      \edef\tempa{\thisrow{#1}}
      \edef\tempb{#2}
      \ifx\tempa\tempb
      \else
      \def\pgfmathresult{inf}
      \fi
    }
  }
}

\begin{document}

            width=\textwidth,
